Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:

   - **Victory Points**: BLUE has 2/10 victory points.
   - **Resources**: BLUE has 2 🌲WOOD, 1 🌾WHEAT.
   - **Development Cards**: BLUE has played 1 KNIGHT card.
   - **Buildings**: BLUE has 2 settlements and 3 roads.
   - **Ports**: The Wood port is at nodes {52, 53}.

3. **Available Actions**:
   - We need to move the robber and potentially steal a resource.
   - The aim is to steal 🧱BRICK to build a road toward the Wood port.

4. **Strategic Considerations**:
   - **Robber Placement**: We need to place the robber on a tile that disrupts RED's resource production and allows us to steal 🧱BRICK.
   - **RED's Settlements**: RED has settlements at nodes 13 and 8. The tiles adjacent to these nodes are:
     - Node 13: 🐑5, 🧱6, 🌾9
     - Node 8: ⛏️9, 🧱5, 🌲11
   - **Potential Steal**: RED has resources from tiles 🧱6, 🧱5, and 🌲11.

5. **Optimal Robber Placement**:
   - To steal 🧱BRICK, we need to place the robber on a tile that produces 🧱BRICK.
   - The tiles producing 🧱BRICK are:
     - (0, -2, 2) producing 🧱3
     - (1, -2, 1) producing 🧱5 (current robber location)
     - (-1, -1, 2) producing 🧱6
   - Moving the robber to (0, -2, 2) will disrupt RED's resource production from the tile producing 🧱3.

6. **Final Decision**:
   - Move the robber to (0, -2, 2) to steal 🧱BRICK from RED and disrupt their resource production.

- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile

- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

RESPONSE:
Given the current game state, let's analyze the best move for the robber to maximize our advantage and potentially hinder the leading player (RED).

### Analysis:

1. **Current Game State:**
   - The robber is currently at (0, -1, 1), blocking a wheat tile.
   - RED has a significant lead with 6 victory points, primarily from their cities.
   - RED's key resource production tiles are:
     - 🧱6 (produces for nodes 16 and 17)
     - ⛏️8 (produces for node 16)
     - 🌲5 (produces for node 16)
     - 🧱9 (produces for node 14)
     - ⛏️5 (produces for node 14)
     - 🐑10 (produces for node 14)

2. **Strategic Considerations:**
   - RED has multiple cities and significant resource production.
   - We need to disrupt RED's resource production to slow their progress.
   - We should avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources we need (wood, since we're building toward the Wood port).

3. **Potential Moves:**
   - Moving the robber to (1, 0, -1) blocks a key ore tile (⛏️8) that produces for RED's city at node 16.
   - Moving the robber to (-1, 1, 0) blocks a key brick tile (🧱6) that produces for RED's cities at nodes 16 and 17.
   - Moving the robber to (1, 1, -2) blocks a key ore tile (⛏️3) that produces for RED's city at node 16.

4. **Evaluation of Moves:**
   - Blocking the ore tile (⛏️8) at (1, 0, -1) is effective but may also hinder our future ore production.
   - Blocking the brick tile (🧱6) at (-1, 1, 0) is highly effective as it disrupts multiple resource productions for RED's key cities.
   - Blocking the ore tile (⛏️3) at (1, 1, -2) is less effective compared to the other options.

### Conclusion:
The best move is to place the robber on the brick tile (🧱6) at (-1, 1, 0) to maximally disrupt RED's resource production.

Mid-Game Resource Management:

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:

1. Think through your decision step by step, analyzing the game state, resources, and available actions
2. Your aim is to WIN. That means 10 victory points.
3. Put your final chosen action inside a box like \\boxed{5}
4. Your final answer must be a single integer corresponding to the action number
5. If you want to create or update your strategic plan, put it in <plan> tags like:
   <plan>Build roads toward port, then build settlement at node 13, then focus on city upgrades</plan>
6. Analyze the recent resource changes to understand what resources you're collecting effectively
7. Think about the next 2-3 turns, not just the immediate action

Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

   - Placing the robber on tiles that produce these resources for RED will disrupt their resource collection.

5. **Best Options**:
   - Option [0]: Move robber to (0, 0, 0) and steal from RED. This tile produces 🐑4, which is useful for RED.
   - Option [3]: Move robber to (-1, 0, 1) and steal from RED. This tile produces 🌲3, which is useful for RED.
   - Option [4]: Move robber to (-1, 1, 0) and steal from RED. This tile produces 🧱12, which is useful for RED.
   - Option [11]: Move robber to (-2, 1, 1) and steal from RED. This tile produces 🧱6, which is useful for RED.

6. **Final Decision**:
   - Option [0] is the best choice because it disrupts RED's 🐑4 production and allows you to steal a resource from RED.

- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

   - Red has settlements at nodes 17 and 20, producing a variety of resources.

   - Blue needs to disrupt Red's resource production to hinder their progress.
   - Red's settlements are at critical resource nodes, especially 🌲WOOD, 🐑SHEEP, and 🧱BRICK.

3. **Potential Moves:**
   - Moving the robber to tiles that produce resources Red is heavily dependent on will be most effective.
   - Tiles to consider:
     - (0, 0, 0) producing 🌲WOOD (3)
     - (1, -1, 0) producing 🌾WHEAT (12)
     - (0, -1, 1) producing 🌾WHEAT (8)
     - (-1, 0, 1) producing 🌲WOOD (10)

     - (1, 1, -2) producing ⛏️ORE (5) and stealing from RED
     - (2, -1, -1) producing ⛏️ORE (11)

4. **Strategic Considerations:**
   - Placing the robber on a tile that produces 🌲WOOD or 🧱BRICK will disrupt Red's ability to build roads and settlements.
   - Stealing a resource from Red will further hinder their progress.
   - Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources Blue is lacking (e.g., 🌾WHEAT).

### Conclusion:

Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- 🔍 marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

Early Game Placement Strategy:
- Aim for a diverse set of resources and strategic road placement.
- Ideal setup: 8-5-10 placement with a secondary placement of 6-9-4 for varied resource collection.
- Avoid being blocked by opponents by securing key roads early.

Mid-Game Resource Management:
- Focus on acquiring necessary resources and engaging in trades with other players.
- Use ports for better trade rates and prioritize building toward ports for better resource management.
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.

Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Prioritize settlements and cities in high victory point locations.
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Effective Trading and Negotiation:
- Actively seek trades with other players using reciprocity and building goodwill.
- Include promises not to place the robber on each other's tiles to make trades more appealing.

Development Card Usage:
- Use development cards strategically to gain an advantage.
- Keep some development cards hidden to deter other players from blocking and stealing.

Robber Placement Strategy:
- Focus on placing the robber on tiles that disrupt the leading player's resource production.
- Avoid placing the robber on tiles that produce resources you are lacking.

   - [10] Move robber to (-2, 0, 2): Not a major resource tile for RED.
   - [11] Move robber to (-2, 1, 1) and steal from RED: Blocks 🐑8, a significant resource tile for RED.
   - [12] Move robber to (-2, 2, 0) and steal from RED: Blocks 🌾5, a significant resource tile for RED.
   - [13] Move robber to (-1, 2, -1) and steal from RED: Not a major resource tile for RED.
   - [14] Move robber to (0, 2, -2): Not a major resource tile for RED.
   - [15] Move robber to (1, 1, -2) and steal from RED: Blocks ⛏️5, a significant resource tile for RED.
   - [16] Move robber to (2, 0, -2): Not a major resource tile for RED.
   - [17] Move robber to (2, -1, -1): Not a major resource tile for RED.

6. **Best Option**:
   - Moving the robber to (1, -1, 0) and stealing from RED (option [1]) is the best move because it blocks 🌾12, a significant resource tile for RED, and allows us to steal a resource from RED.

Final chosen action:
